# Global functions

The following content is in MediaWiki markdown format:

```mediawiki
{{uitech|doc=}} {{for|{{Wow-inline}} Classic functions|Global functions/Classic}}
This page contains ''automatically generated'' and alphabetically sorted lists of global functions usable in the World of Warcraft scripting engine. Its main purpose is to be an authoritative (insofar that this is possible) list of what functions actually exist. For short descriptions of what the API functions do, see [[World of Warcraft API]]; API changes observed in major patches are also noted in [[API change summaries]].
```
